function kiyaslaUrunKodlarAlSuccess(result) {
var urn_kodList = "";
var urn_kodlar = "";

if (urn_kodList.split(':').length > 1) {
urn_kodlar = urn_kodList.split(':')[1];
}

{
urn_kodlar = urn_kodlar.substring(urn_kodlar.length - 1 ,0);
var kiyasUrl = "/urun_kiyaslama.aspx";
kiyasUrl = kiyasUrl.replace("$kodlar$",'&uKods='+urn_kodlar);
window.location.href = kiyasUrl;
}
else
alert($("span[id$='lbfKIYASLAMA_VLD']").html());
}

var strMsgEmailMesaj = $('#' + ascBultenObjID + '_lbfEMAIL_MESAJ').html();
if (strMsgEmailMesaj !== '') {
var strUyeMail = $('#' + ascBultenObjID + '_txtUYE_EMAIL');
strUyeMail.val(strMsgEmailMesaj);
strUyeMail.blur(function () {
if ($(this).val() === '') {
$(this).val(strMsgEmailMesaj);
}
});
strUyeMail.focus(function () {
if ($(this).val() === strMsgEmailMesaj) {
$(this).val('');
}
});
}
function bultenKaydet()
{           
BultenMailGonder();
}
function BultenMailGonder() {
var strMsgEmailMesaj = $("#" + ascBultenObjID + "_lbfEMAIL_MESAJ").html();
var email = $("#aspnetForm #" + ascBultenObjID + "_txtUYE_EMAIL");
var sending = $("#" + ascBultenObjID + "_lblHBB_GONDERILIYOR");
if (email.val() !== "" && email.val() !== strMsgEmailMesaj) {
sending.html("");
if (checkEmail(email.val())) {
sending.html($("#" + ascBultenObjID + "_lbfHBB_GONDERILIYOR").html());
pageMethod("/pageMethods.aspx/bultenKaydet", '{"strEmail":"' + email.val() + '", "lngCultureName": "tr-TR"}', function success(result) {
if (result.d === "")
sending.html(strHBB_GONDERILIYOR_BASARILI);
else
sending.html(strHBB_GONDERILIYOR_BASARISIZ);
if (typeof stage !== 'undefined') stage.dispatchEvent("CustomEvent", "eBultenResult");
}, function error(result) {
sending.html(strHBB_GONDERILIYOR_BASARISIZ); if (typeof stage !== 'undefined') stage.dispatchEvent("CustomEvent", "eBultenResult");
console.log(result.d);
});
email.val('');
}
}
else
{
var strHBB_BOSGECILEMEZ = $("#" + ascBultenObjID + "_lbfHBB_BOSGECILEMEZ").html();
alert(strHBB_BOSGECILEMEZ);
return false;
}
}
